commit 700c125900a0f92d0dfa11a8840e6d7b7b3ca263
Author: Mirko Friedenhagen <mfriedenhagen@apache.org>
Date:   Wed Mar 25 21:18:36 2015 +0000

    Add a solution for running org.apache.maven.shared.release.exec.InvokerMavenExecutorTest.
    
    The Maven shell scripts do not export M2_HOME correctly. The system property maven.home
    is not inherited by default in surefire. Directly setting maven.home here does not work
    because a lot of the tests are checking M2_HOME.
    So introduce a system property injectedMavenHome in surefire which is picked up by
    InvokerMavenExecutorTest lateron to determine maven.home.
    
    
    git-svn-id: https://svn.apache.org/repos/asf/maven/release/trunk@1669230 13f79535-47bb-0310-9956-ffa450edef68

commit 8df63b121565699d1238c4fcd937357cc7dbceb9
Author: Mark Struberg <struberg@apache.org>

    MRELEASE-727 only parse for the pom directory if the SCM itself doesn't know
    
    If the SCM can provide a relativePath then we take this info.
    Otherwise we scan all subdirs until we found the pom in question.

    as they don't have the concept of a 'sparse' checkout.

commit 33a3700ab35a283f41229590bdad088a622e1768
Author: Stephen Connolly <stephenc@apache.org>
Date:   Fri Jun 24 15:48:07 2011 +0000

    [MRELEASE-159] Support a pattern to generate the release tag.
    
    o I had a quick look at the suggested solutions and basing off of MessageFormat requires people to remember exactly which {0} and {1} correspond with. This solution uses plexus-interpolation to interpolate properties delimited with @{ and } so that the properties escape Maven's default interpolation which would resolve them in the -SNAPSHOT project.
    
    o May need to double check that the site generates correctly

commit b710a019abbc6d844f7299f557308e0fc617bf1c
Author: Mark Struberg <struberg@apache.org>
Date:   Thu Dec 23 22:42:35 2010 +0000

    MRELEASE-457 Non sparse-checkout SCM support
    
    If a SCM system doesn't support sparse checkout (like GIT, hg, etc),
    maven did fail to pickup the 'right' child module from
    target/checkout. This patch automatically searches for this
    'right' child project and sets the checkoutPath for all further
    tasks accordingly.
